\subsubsection{MandateEpoch Protocol: Scaling Real Multi-Agent Work
Without Putting Every Microjob
On-Chain}\label{mandateepoch-protocol-scaling-real-multi-agent-work-without-putting-every-microjob-on-chain}

A market-governed invention engine should not create one on-chain job
for every invention microstep. One AGIJobManager job should represent
one \textbf{MandateEpoch}, while NettingHouse batches high-volume
invention receipts off-chain and commits settlement-grade roots.

A mandate is:

\[
\begin{aligned}
M = (&\mathrm{goal}, \mathrm{budget}, \mathrm{policy},
\mathrm{descriptor\_schema}, \mathrm{scoring\_rubric},\\
&\mathrm{safety\_policy}, \mathrm{validator\_policy},
\mathrm{promotion\_thresholds}, \mathrm{reinvestment\_policy}).
\end{aligned}
\]

A MandateEpoch is:

\[
\begin{aligned}
E_t = (&\mathrm{mandate\_id}, \mathrm{epoch\_id}, \mathrm{policy\_hash},
\mathrm{descriptor\_schema\_hash},\\
&\mathrm{score\_rubric\_hash}, \mathrm{safety\_policy\_hash},
\mathrm{validator\_policy\_hash},\\
&\mathrm{receipt\_root}, \mathrm{payout\_root},
\mathrm{archive\_delta\_root}, \mathrm{quarantine\_root},\\
&\mathrm{validator\_attestation\_bundle}, \mathrm{challenge\_window},
\mathrm{payout\_budget}, \mathrm{metadata\_uri}).
\end{aligned}
\]

The microjob alphabet is:

\begin{Shaded}
\begin{Highlighting}[]
\NormalTok{PROPOSE, CAUSALIZE, SCORE\_FAST, SCORE\_LCM, NOVELTY, REDTEAM,}
\NormalTok{ARCHIVE\_INSERT, VALIDATE\_REPLAY, PROMOTE\_CANDIDATE,}
\NormalTok{PACKAGE\_CAPABILITY, UPDATE\_INSIGHT\_SIGNAL}
\end{Highlighting}
\end{Shaded}

Inside each epoch, NettingHouse authorizes microjobs, Alpha-Factory runs
the invention swarm, the causal-substrate service evaluates mechanism
plausibility and side effects, the QD archive stores elites and stepping
stones, restricted-domain routing and red-team gates quarantine unsafe
candidates, NettingHouse commits receipt, archive-delta, payout, and
quarantine roots, OpenClaw reviewers inspect promotions and quarantines,
and AGIJobManager validates or finalizes the epoch as the authoritative
settlement checkpoint. ProofBundles and alpha-WU records are exported at
epoch finalization.

The epoch-level flow is:

\begin{Shaded}
\begin{Highlighting}[]
\NormalTok{Sponsor mandate}
\NormalTok{{-}\textgreater{} Paymaster opens epoch}
\NormalTok{{-}\textgreater{} NettingHouse authorizes microjobs}
\NormalTok{{-}\textgreater{} Alpha{-}Factory runs invention swarm}
\NormalTok{{-}\textgreater{} causal substrate evaluates mechanism plausibility and side effects}
\NormalTok{{-}\textgreater{} QD archive stores elites and stepping stones}
\NormalTok{{-}\textgreater{} restricted{-}domain router and red{-}team gate unsafe candidates}
\NormalTok{{-}\textgreater{} NettingHouse commits receipt\_root / archive\_delta\_root / payout\_root}
\NormalTok{   and quarantine\_root}
\NormalTok{{-}\textgreater{} OpenClaw reviewer inspects quarantine and promotion candidates}
\NormalTok{{-}\textgreater{} AGIJobManager validates/finalizes epoch}
\NormalTok{{-}\textgreater{} settlement, alpha{-}WU accounting, ProofBundle export}
\NormalTok{{-}\textgreater{} capability package / invention reserve / reinvestment update}
\NormalTok{{-}\textgreater{} next harder mandate}
\end{Highlighting}
\end{Shaded}

\subsubsection{Global QD Backbone: Stepping-Stone Preservation as System
State}\label{global-qd-backbone-stepping-stone-preservation-as-system-state}

AGI ALPHA must not treat quality diversity as a side module. The global
QD archive is the memory of open-ended invention. It stores diverse,
high-quality stepping stones across tasks, environments, agent
workflows, validators, causal mechanisms, Nova-Seed-like foresight
artifacts, capability packages, and market designs.

For descriptor cell \(d\):

\[
\mathrm{ArchiveCell}[d]
=
\text{best known validated artifact in descriptor cell } d.
\]

The archive admits multiple artifact classes: invention candidates, task
environments, agent workflows, validators, tool contracts, market
mechanisms, causal motifs, software patches, scientific hypotheses,
capability packages, foresight artifacts, proof templates, operator
playbooks, and reinvestment strategies.

A descriptor schema for invention throughput contains:

\begin{Shaded}
\begin{Highlighting}[]
\NormalTok{D1 prototype cost}
\NormalTok{D2 time{-}to{-}prototype}
\NormalTok{D3 deployment surface}
\NormalTok{D4 coordination complexity}
\NormalTok{D5 modality}
\NormalTok{D6 dependency intensity}
\NormalTok{D7 domain entropy / cross{-}domain recombination}
\NormalTok{D8 regulatory or compliance friction}
\NormalTok{D9 verification difficulty}
\NormalTok{D10 reinvestment relevance}
\NormalTok{D11 compute or energy leverage}
\NormalTok{D12 safety / reversibility class}
\end{Highlighting}
\end{Shaded}

The score vector is written compactly as:

\[
s(x)=(F,C,I,N,R,T,S,V,E).
\]

Here \(F\) is feasibility, \(C\) causal coherence, \(I\) impact
potential, \(N\) mechanism novelty, \(R\) robustness, \(T\) testability,
\(S\) safety margin, \(V\) reinvestment value, and \(E\)
compute-or-energy leverage.

A scalar quality proxy is:

\[
\begin{aligned}
Q(x)=&
0.16F + 0.16C + 0.15I + 0.13N\\
&+0.10R + 0.10T + 0.08S + 0.07V + 0.05E,
\end{aligned}
\]

where \(F\) is feasibility, \(C\) causal coherence, \(I\) impact
potential, \(N\) mechanism novelty, \(R\) robustness, \(T\) testability,
\(S\) safety margin, \(V\) reinvestment value, and \(E\)
compute-or-energy leverage.

Safety is not merely a score. It is a gate.

\begin{Shaded}
\begin{Highlighting}[]
\NormalTok{RiskTier in \{ALLOW, CAUTION, RESTRICTED, PROHIBITED\}}
\NormalTok{Red{-}team verdict in \{ALLOW, ALLOW\_WITH\_CONSTRAINTS, RESTRICT, PROHIBIT\}}
\end{Highlighting}
\end{Shaded}

A candidate may be promoted only if it is ALLOW, or CAUTION with
red-team approval; feasibility, causal coherence, testability, and
safety margin are all at least 4 on the relevant rubric; replayability
passes; the ProofBundle is complete; and at least one of impact
potential, mechanism novelty, or reinvestment value is at least 4.
PROHIBITED artifacts are dropped except for a minimal hash, reason code,
and safety category. RESTRICTED artifacts are quarantined and never
auto-promoted.

\subsubsection{Causal Substrate for Invention
Search}\label{causal-substrate-for-invention-search}

Foundation models and QD archives make invention searchable. A causal
substrate makes the search mechanism-level rather than word-level. AGI
ALPHA defines its own commercially independent causal-substrate service
rather than depending on any external causal-model implementation.

A causal slice is:

\[
\mathrm{CausalSlice}=(D,G,M,L,P,\Gamma,V,I_{\mathrm{known}},S_{\mathrm{effects}}).
\]

The tuple records domain, causal graph, manifold embedding, cross-slice
links, provenance, confidence, version, known interventions, and known
side effects.

The causal-substrate service exposes the following AGI ALPHA-native
APIs:

\begin{Shaded}
\begin{Highlighting}[]
\NormalTok{neighbors(node, k, slice)}
\NormalTok{bridge(query\_nodes, target\_slice)}
\NormalTok{mechanism\_check(chain)}
\NormalTok{intervention\_sketch(do(X))}
\NormalTok{side\_effect\_scan(intervention, risk\_taxonomy)}
\NormalTok{novelty\_density(node\_or\_chain)}
\NormalTok{active\_deepen(frontier\_region, uncertainty\_budget)}
\NormalTok{counterfactual\_probe(candidate, alternative\_conditions)}
\end{Highlighting}
\end{Shaded}

Active deepening spends causal-modeling budget only where the QD
frontier indicates high uncertainty, high novelty, high value, or high
risk. This prevents the system from wasting expensive modeling effort on
low-value regions while preserving the ability to inspect high-impact
mechanisms before promotion.

\subsubsection{OpenClaw as Operator Shell, Not Source of
Truth}\label{openclaw-as-operator-shell-not-source-of-truth}

OpenClaw is not the scheduler, settlement source, or archive source of
truth. It is the human-facing control shell for sponsors, reviewers, and
operators.

\textbf{SponsorClaw} creates mandates, opens epochs, inspects archives,
adjusts budgets, approves promotion classes, views flywheel
contribution, and reviews reinvestment options.

\textbf{ReviewerClaw} inspects quarantine, reviews red-team rationales,
inspects causal chains, approves constrained candidates, requires
additional validation, and blocks unsafe promotion.

\textbf{OperatorClaw} monitors epoch health, inspects failed receipts,
reruns verification, submits epoch roots, validates or finalizes epoch
jobs, inspects node telemetry, and triggers fail-closed controls.

OpenClaw skills include:

\begin{Shaded}
\begin{Highlighting}[]
\NormalTok{create\_mandate}
\NormalTok{open\_epoch}
\NormalTok{inspect\_archive\_cell}
\NormalTok{inspect\_quarantine}
\NormalTok{approve\_restricted\_candidate}
\NormalTok{request\_extra\_validation}
\NormalTok{validate\_epoch}
\NormalTok{finalize\_epoch}
\NormalTok{promote\_to\_alpha\_factory}
\NormalTok{export\_public\_proof\_pack}
\NormalTok{export\_private\_audit\_pack}
\end{Highlighting}
\end{Shaded}

The AGIJobManager adapter exposes:

\begin{Shaded}
\begin{Highlighting}[]
\NormalTok{open\_epoch\_job(mandateId, epochId, payoutBudget, metadataURI)}
\NormalTok{commit\_epoch\_root(epochId, receiptRoot, archiveDeltaRoot, attestationBundle)}
\NormalTok{validate\_epoch\_job(epochId)}
\NormalTok{finalize\_epoch\_job(epochId)}
\NormalTok{open\_dispute(epochId, receiptId)}
\NormalTok{publish\_chronicle\_entry(epochId)}
\end{Highlighting}
\end{Shaded}

The metadata URI must point to an epoch bundle containing mandate policy
hash, descriptor schema hash, scoring rubric hash, safety policy hash,
validator policy hash, receipt root, payout root, archive delta root,
quarantine root, red-team summary statistics, restricted-domain
escalations, payout totals, validator attestation bundle, replay and
audit artifacts, public-safe report, and private audit appendix.

\subsubsection{AGI Nodes as Verifiable Open-Ended
Compute}\label{agi-nodes-as-verifiable-open-ended-compute}

AGI Nodes do not reduce the total compute required for open-ended QD or
AI-generating search. They increase available compute supply, distribute
embarrassingly parallel work, and allocate compute toward validated
search objectives. Frontier-model pretraining requires tightly coupled,
high-bandwidth clusters and is not solved by ordinary decentralized
nodes. Open-ended invention search is different: candidate generation,
evaluation, novelty scoring, archive maintenance, replay, red-team, and
validation are naturally parallelizable and can be distributed across
AGI Nodes.

AGI Nodes therefore solve the second bottleneck now and support the
first indirectly through data generation, evaluation, distillation,
fine-tuning, and hyperparameter search.

Node job types include:

\begin{Shaded}
\begin{Highlighting}[]
\NormalTok{WU\_ENV\_MUTATE}
\NormalTok{WU\_INTERESTINGNESS}
\NormalTok{WU\_SOLVE\_ATTEMPT}
\NormalTok{WU\_EVAL\_ROLLOUT}
\NormalTok{WU\_NOVELTY}
\NormalTok{WU\_CAUSALIZE}
\NormalTok{WU\_ARCHIVE\_PROPOSE}
\NormalTok{WU\_ARCHIVE\_MAINTAIN}
\NormalTok{WU\_REDTEAM}
\NormalTok{WU\_VALIDATE\_REPLAY}
\NormalTok{WU\_PACKAGE\_CAPABILITY}
\end{Highlighting}
\end{Shaded}

The verification ladder is:

\begin{itemize}
\tightlist
\item
  \textbf{L0:} syntax, schema, and hash checks.
\item
  \textbf{L1:} deterministic replay from container hash, environment
  hash, dependency pins, and seeds.
\item
  \textbf{L2:} redundant execution for high-value or disputed work.
\item
  \textbf{L3:} audit sampling and challenge games for routine work.
\item
  \textbf{L4:} TEE, zkML, or cryptographic proof only where economically
  justified.
\item
  \textbf{L5:} human or institutional escalation for high-impact,
  irreversible, or legally sensitive actions.
\end{itemize}

No compute reward is released without a replayable receipt, validator
attestation, and challenge window.

\subsubsection{Economics of Open-Ended Search: Funding Compute Without
Speculative
Dependence}\label{economics-of-open-ended-search-funding-compute-without-speculative-dependence}

Open-ended invention search needs funding, but the protocol must remain
legally and commercially conservative. AGI ALPHA defines the
\textbf{Alpha Foundry Mandate Facility} (\(\alpha\mathrm{FMF}\)) as a
utility-only funding and clearing facility for invention-search mandates
while preserving strict \$AGIALPHA-denominated settlement. It is not
equity, not debt, not profit-sharing, not yield-bearing, not a security,
and not a promise of operator profit. It is a utility clearing facility
for funding, pricing, metering, and settling AGI ALPHA work.

Components include Mandate Registry, budget account or endowment vault,
AGIALPHA Paymaster, Redemption Window with caps and spreads where
applicable, Epoch NettingHouse, Coverage Ratio Controller, Archive
Registry, Causal Slice Registry, Policy Gate, and operator risk ledger.

Coverage is:

\[
\mathrm{CoverageRatio}
=
\frac{R_{\mathrm{stable}}+R_{\mathrm{liquid}}}
{E_{\mathrm{redeem}}+E_{\mathrm{bounty}}+E_{\mathrm{reserve}}}.
\]

Here \(R_{\mathrm{stable}}\) and \(R_{\mathrm{liquid}}\) are reserve and
inventory terms, while \(E_{\mathrm{redeem}}\), \(E_{\mathrm{bounty}}\),
and \(E_{\mathrm{reserve}}\) are expected redemption, bounty-pipeline,
and operating-reserve requirements.

Throttle rules are simple. Healthy coverage permits normal QD and
invention search. Moderate coverage throttles exploratory jobs first.
Low coverage continues paid customer jobs, validation, and dispute
resolution while pausing noncritical exploration. Critical coverage
pauses new mandates and preserves settlement, auditability, and
disputes.

Compute pricing is:

\[
\mathrm{Escrow}_{\mathrm{AGIALPHA}}
\ge
\frac{
\mathrm{ACU}\cdot \mathrm{USD}_{\mathrm{ACU}}\cdot
(1+\mathrm{margin}+\mathrm{risk}+\mathrm{verification})
}{
\mathrm{AGIALPHA}_{\mathrm{USD}}\cdot
\mathrm{operator\_net\_share}
}.
\]

Risk-adjusted operator economics are:

\[
\begin{aligned}
\Pi_{\mathrm{op}}=&\ P_{\mathrm{net}}
-C_{\mathrm{compute}}
-C_{\mathrm{energy}}
-C_{\mathrm{hardware}}\\
&-C_{\mathrm{api}}
-L_{\mathrm{slash}}
-C_{\mathrm{liquidity}}
-C_{\mathrm{opportunity}}.
\end{aligned}
\]

Here \(\Pi_{\mathrm{op}}\) is expected operator profit under stated
assumptions.

with:

\[
\mathrm{ExpectedSlashLoss}
=
p_{\mathrm{failure}}\cdot
\mathrm{slash\_fraction}\cdot
\mathrm{stake\_at\_risk}.
\]

A node workload is admitted only if expected operator profit is positive
under stated assumptions, but the paper must not present this as
guaranteed operator profit. The protocol cannot make node economics work
by assertion; it must show that bounties, validator overhead, slashing
risk, liquidity constraints, and compute costs can balance under
realistic workload assumptions.

\subsubsection{alpha-AGI Insight: Real Jobs as Foresight
Signals}\label{alpha-agi-insight-real-jobs-as-foresight-signals}

alpha-AGI Insight should not claim perfect foresight. Its defensible
claim is that running real AGI Jobs at scale reveals \textbf{stepping
stones}: repeated proof-bearing patterns that indicate where machine
labor is producing compounding leverage.

A stepping stone is:

\[
\begin{aligned}
\mathrm{SteppingStone}=(&\mathrm{task\_family}, \mathrm{validated\_artifact},
\mathrm{reusable\_capability}, \mathrm{cost\_reduction},\\
&\mathrm{transfer\_score}, \mathrm{lineage\_pointer},
\mathrm{sector\_signal}, \mathrm{risk\_profile},\\
&\mathrm{reinvestment\_option}, \mathrm{evidence\_bundle\_pointer}).
\end{aligned}
\]

A sector insight score is:

\[
\mathrm{InsightScore}(s)
=
\frac{
f_s\cdot r_s\cdot c_s\cdot t_s\cdot k_s\cdot e_s
}{
\rho_s+\ell_s+v_s+u_s
},
\]

where \(f_s\) is frequency of validated stepping stones, \(r_s\)
reusability, \(c_s\) cost decline, \(t_s\) transferability, \(k_s\)
capitalizability, \(e_s\) infrastructure-compute-energy relevance,
\(\rho_s\) risk, \(\ell_s\) regulatory friction, \(v_s\) validator
burden, and \(u_s\) uncertainty.

AGI ALPHA should discover high-value opportunity regions by executing
increasingly demanding AGI Jobs and observing which validated stepping
stones repeatedly compound. The paper must avoid claims of pinpoint
certainty, guaranteed optimal opportunities, achieved superintelligence,
guaranteed market dominance, or deterministic future prediction. The
claim is structured foresight through validated work: machine-speed
weak-signal discovery, evidence-grounded opportunity mapping, and
increasingly precise sector signals.

\subsubsection{Real-Task Demonstration: Scalable, Efficient, Safe
Coordination}\label{real-task-demonstration-scalable-efficient-safe-coordination}

This section is mandatory for turning the paper from architecture into
science. It separates three claims.

\textbf{Scalability.} Does adding agents, tools, validators, memory,
routing, and nodes improve throughput or task coverage without exploding
coordination overhead?

\textbf{Efficiency.} Does the system produce more verified work per unit
of compute, token spend, wall-clock time, tool call, or human review
than simpler baselines?

\textbf{Safety.} Does the system maintain policy, security, privacy,
reversibility, process integrity, and subversion resistance on realistic
tasks?

The minimum public evidence bundle for any coordination claim contains:

\begin{Shaded}
\begin{Highlighting}[]
\NormalTok{public task ID or job spec}
\NormalTok{task manifest}
\NormalTok{agent constellation and role contracts}
\NormalTok{router decision}
\NormalTok{tool{-}call trace}
\NormalTok{handoff trace}
\NormalTok{artifacts}
\NormalTok{validator report}
\NormalTok{red{-}team report where applicable}
\NormalTok{cost ledger}
\NormalTok{safety ledger}
\NormalTok{settlement receipt or clearly labeled simulated settlement receipt}
\NormalTok{replay instructions}
\NormalTok{failure cases}
\NormalTok{baseline comparison}
\NormalTok{repeated{-}trial reliability estimate}
\end{Highlighting}
\end{Shaded}

No cherry-picked demo, private-only trace, unreplayable run, hidden
human intervention, fake completion URI, or synthetic proof may be
counted as demonstrated coordination.

The evidence plan has three stages.

\textbf{Stage A: Single MandateEpoch proof pack.} Run one real,
replayable task end-to-end: job spec -\textgreater{} routed agents
-\textgreater{} bounded tools -\textgreater{} validator -\textgreater{}
ProofBundle -\textgreater{} NettingHouse receipt -\textgreater{}
OpenClaw review -\textgreater{} AGIJobManager-compatible settlement
artifact.

\textbf{Stage B: Baseline benchmark.} Compare B0-B5 under equal
model/tool/budget constraints on software repair, web/API workflow,
policy-bound tool use, scientific/data workflow, and one AGI Jobs
protocol-native task.

\textbf{Stage C: Scaling curve.} Run the same task families with 1, 2,
4, 8, and 16 agents and with local versus distributed node execution.
Measure throughput, verified work per cost, validator overhead,
coordination overhead, failure recovery, and safety incidents.

\subsubsection{Commercial independence and claim
boundary}\label{commercial-independence-and-claim-boundary}

ALPHA-AGI Insight v02 is used as an internal strategic and technical
architecture brief. External works discussed in that brief, including
quality-diversity, open-ended search, AI feedback, causal-model
extraction, and agentic-system design, are cited only as scientific
inspiration and prior-art context. AGI ALPHA develops its own
commercially independent mechanisms: MandateEpochs, ProofBundles,
alpha-Work Units, NettingHouse batching, Paymaster funding,
AGIJobManager settlement adapters, OpenClaw operator skills, AGI.Eth
identity, Alpha-Factory invention workflows, causal-substrate services,
safety gates, QD archives, verifiable distributed compute, and
value-to-energy reinvestment governance.

The paper does not claim that AGI ALPHA has already achieved
superintelligence, autonomous economic sovereignty, energy abundance, or
civilization-scale capability. It claims that a market-governed,
proof-gated, causally informed, QD-driven intelligence-organization
substrate is a plausible architecture for testing whether verified
machine labor can compound into reusable capability, capital,
infrastructure, compute, science, and useful-energy capacity. The claim
becomes empirical only through MandateEpoch results, real-task
benchmarks, replayable proof bundles, validator audits, safety ledgers,
delayed outcomes, baseline comparisons, and cost/risk accounting.

\subsection{AGI Alpha RSI: Sovereign Invention Governance for Recursive
Self-Improving Machine
Labor}\label{agi-alpha-rsi-sovereign-invention-governance-for-recursive-self-improving-machine-labor}

AGI Alpha RSI is the deterministic sovereign governance control plane
inside AGI ALPHA. AGI ALPHA is the scalable substrate for intelligence
organizations; AGI Alpha RSI is the deterministic governance institution
for recursive self-improving invention. Together, they transform
open-ended discovery from a novelty process into an auditable,
replayable, baseline-comparative, value-producing institution.

AGI Alpha RSI is a deterministic invention operating system for
open-ended discovery, governed deployment, and compounding advantage.
Its purpose is to build the governance institution first, before
AGI-scale systems mature. It is not a novelty mill, hype engine, or
black-box outcome authority. It is a control architecture where
breakthroughs are admitted only as audited state transitions. The
internal RSI materials define the kernel as deterministic invention
operations with schema-bound artifacts, baseline-comparative evaluation,
ECI semantics, Move-37 handling, replayability, and mandatory dossier
packaging {[}90-92{]}.

\textbf{RSI design invariant.} Exploration is allowed. Outcome authority
is mechanical. Promotion requires evidence. Compounding requires
persistence. Autonomy requires authority.

OMNI-style interestingness provides search control, not outcome
authority. Interestingness may influence allocation, targeting, and
exploration pressure, but it must never override risk gates, executed
evidence, baseline comparison, persistence tests, replay, validator
authority, or settlement rules.

\begin{figure}
\centering
\includegraphics[width=0.96\textwidth,height=\textheight]{figures_png/figure30_rsi_control_plane.png}
\caption{AGI Alpha RSI deterministic governance control plane. TARGET
-\textgreater{} EMIT -\textgreater{} FILTER -\textgreater{} ATLAS
-\textgreater{} TEST-PLAN -\textgreater{} EVAL -\textgreater{} INSERT
-\textgreater{} PROMOTE is wrapped by replay integrity, ECI evidence
discipline, and mechanical outcome authority.}
\end{figure}

\subsubsection{RSI pipeline formalism}\label{rsi-pipeline-formalism}

The RSI cycle is:

\[
\boxed{
\mathrm{TARGET}
\rightarrow
\mathrm{EMIT}
\rightarrow
\mathrm{FILTER}
\rightarrow
\mathrm{ATLAS}
\rightarrow
\mathrm{TEST\text{-}PLAN}
\rightarrow
\mathrm{EVAL}
\rightarrow
\mathrm{INSERT}
\rightarrow
\mathrm{PROMOTE}
}
\]

\begin{longtable}[]{@{}
  >{\raggedright\arraybackslash}p{(\columnwidth - 2\tabcolsep) * \real{0.5000}}
  >{\raggedright\arraybackslash}p{(\columnwidth - 2\tabcolsep) * \real{0.5000}}@{}}
\toprule\noalign{}
\begin{minipage}[b]{\linewidth}\raggedright
Stage
\end{minipage} & \begin{minipage}[b]{\linewidth}\raggedright
Function
\end{minipage} \\
\midrule\noalign{}
\endhead
\bottomrule\noalign{}
\endlastfoot
TARGET & Allocate exploration pressure across archive cells, bridge
regions, themes, open-ended environments, task families, and strategic
mandates. \\
EMIT & Generate candidate artifacts, agent lineages, workflows,
environments, validators, scaffolds, causal hypotheses, or invention
candidates. \\
FILTER & Apply risk gating, prohibited-domain detection, novelty and
boringness checks, OMNI interestingness, and routing decisions: reject,
probe, refine, escalate, or continue. \\
ATLAS & Extract causal triples, mechanism chains, contradictions, side
effects, bridge hypotheses, and cross-domain causal links. \\
TEST-PLAN & Build falsification ladders and microbench plans using
uncertainty focus, expected information gain, and cheapest-valid-probe
scheduling. \\
EVAL & Run baseline-comparative evaluations, deterministic microbenches,
external validators, executed evidence, cost/risk ledgers, and ECI
updates. \\
INSERT & Update MAP-Elites / QD archive mechanically under descriptor
cells, evidence thresholds, replayability, and safety gates. \\
PROMOTE & Rank candidates for deployment, deeper testing, capability
packaging, MandateEpoch settlement, invention reserve inclusion, or
reinvestment. \\
\end{longtable}

\subsubsection{RSI state object and persistence
invariants}\label{rsi-state-object-and-persistence-invariants}

The RSI state is a schema-bound, append-only institutional memory
object:

\[
\begin{aligned}
\mathrm{RSIState}_t = (&
\mathrm{cycle\_index},
\mathrm{prompt\_pack\_hash},
\mathrm{runner\_config\_hash},
\mathrm{state\_payload\_hash},\\
&\mathrm{archive},
\mathrm{scaffolds},
\mathrm{candidates},
\mathrm{causal\_atlas},
\mathrm{eci\_ledger},
\mathrm{evidence\_objects},\\
&\mathrm{baseline\_library},
\mathrm{proof\_bundles},
\mathrm{promotion\_queue},
\mathrm{dossier\_index},
\mathrm{safety\_ledger},\\
&\mathrm{drift\_sentinel},
\mathrm{governance\_state})
\end{aligned}
\]

Persistence invariants:

\begin{enumerate}
\def\labelenumi{\arabic{enumi}.}
\tightlist
\item
  \texttt{cycle\_index} increments exactly +1 on continuation runs.
\item
  \texttt{archive.candidates} is append-only.
\item
  \texttt{archive.scaffolds} is append-only.
\item
  \texttt{causal\_atlas.triples} is append-only.
\item
  \texttt{eci.ledger} is append-only.
\item
  Occupied frontier cells are non-decreasing unless a signed
  archive-reorganization event is emitted.
\item
  \texttt{prompt\_pack\_hash}, \texttt{runner\_config\_hash}, and
  \texttt{state\_payload\_hash} are bound into the next state.
\item
  No runner may silently reinitialize state.
\item
  If state cannot be verified, the runner must halt rather than
  continue.
\item
  If drift is intentional, it must use an explicit signed drift
  override.
\end{enumerate}

\subsubsection{Deterministic Drift Sentinel and Replay
Integrity}\label{deterministic-drift-sentinel-and-replay-integrity}

AGI Alpha RSI makes recursive improvement underwritable by refusing to
proceed when inputs or state drift silently. The drift sentinel
computes:

\[
\begin{aligned}
h_p &= \mathrm{SHA256}(\mathrm{canonical\_json}(\mathrm{prompt\_pack})),\\
h_r &= \mathrm{SHA256}(\mathrm{canonical\_json}(\mathrm{runner\_config})),\\
h_s &= \mathrm{SHA256}(\mathrm{canonical\_json}(\mathrm{state}^{\oslash})).
\end{aligned}
\]

Here, \(\mathrm{state}^{\oslash}\) denotes the state after setting
\texttt{state\_manifest.state\_payload\_hash\ =\ null} and excluding
explicit drift-override acknowledgement fields from the hash
calculation.

\textbf{Run rule.} Before each RSI cycle, compute all three hashes. If
any mismatch occurs without an authorized drift override, the runner
hard-fails, outputs a run manifest, leaves state unchanged, and does not
mutate the archive, atlas, ECI ledger, scaffolds, or cycle index.

Hard-fail conditions include prompt pack drift, runner config drift,
state payload corruption, cycle index reset, archive shrinkage, scaffold
shrinkage, causal atlas shrinkage, ECI ledger shrinkage, unexplained
schema change, unexplained prompt change, or unexplained scoring change.
A recursively improving system without drift detection is not
underwritable; it is a prompt loop with memory risk.

\subsubsection{Evidence Contact Index: confidence cannot inflate without
execution}\label{evidence-contact-index-confidence-cannot-inflate-without-execution}

The Evidence Contact Index (ECI) is an AGI ALPHA-native evidence-contact
measure. It prevents simulated reasoning from being mistaken for
executed, replayed, stress-tested, or externally validated evidence.

\begin{longtable}[]{@{}
  >{\raggedright\arraybackslash}p{(\columnwidth - 4\tabcolsep) * \real{0.3333}}
  >{\raggedright\arraybackslash}p{(\columnwidth - 4\tabcolsep) * \real{0.3333}}
  >{\raggedright\arraybackslash}p{(\columnwidth - 4\tabcolsep) * \real{0.3333}}@{}}
\toprule\noalign{}
\begin{minipage}[b]{\linewidth}\raggedright
Level
\end{minipage} & \begin{minipage}[b]{\linewidth}\raggedright
Meaning
\end{minipage} & \begin{minipage}[b]{\linewidth}\raggedright
Promotion implication
\end{minipage} \\
\midrule\noalign{}
\endhead
\bottomrule\noalign{}
\endlastfoot
E0 SIMULATED & LLM-only reasoning, scenario generation, or internal
judgment. & Cannot push ECI beyond a low cap. \\
E1 PROBED & Deterministic syntactic, schema, static-analysis, or cheap
microbench check. & Allows probe status only. \\
E2 EXECUTED & Candidate run in sandbox, container, benchmark, test
harness, tool environment, or microbench with logged outputs. & Required
for promotion beyond probe status. \\
E3 REPLAYED & Independent replay reproduces the result from pinned
seeds, container hashes, dependency pins, and manifest. & Required for
settlement-grade claims. \\
E4 STRESS-TESTED & Candidate retains advantage under policy shocks,
adversarial perturbations, alternative seeds, nearby baselines, and
failure-mode probes. & Required for high-novelty candidates. \\
E5 EXTERNALLY VALIDATED & External validator, real-world outcome, human
expert, independent lab, market settlement, or delayed outcome confirms
result. & Required for strong empirical claims. \\
\end{longtable}

Let \(\mathrm{ECI}(x)\in[0,1]\). Confidence cannot inflate without
executed or replayed evidence. Priority is therefore:

\[
\begin{aligned}
\mathrm{Priority}(x)=&
\ \mathrm{Interestingness}(x)
\cdot (1-\mathrm{ECI}_{\mathrm{uncertainty}}(x))\\
&\cdot \mathrm{BaselineOutperformanceValue}(x)
\cdot \mathrm{MissionUtility}(x)\\
&\cdot \mathrm{SafetyGate}(x)
\cdot \mathrm{Replayability}(x),
\end{aligned}
\]

with \(\mathrm{SafetyGate}(x)=0\) for prohibited or critical-risk
candidates.

\subsubsection{Move-37 breakthrough handling: high novelty implies
higher
skepticism}\label{move-37-breakthrough-handling-high-novelty-implies-higher-skepticism}

A breakthrough is not a story. It is a deterministic state transition.
The RSI trigger is:

\[
\begin{aligned}
\mathrm{Move37Candidate}(x)=1
\quad\mathrm{iff}\quad&
\mathrm{NoveltyDistance}(x)\geq\tau_{\mathrm{novelty}}\\
&\wedge\ \mathrm{AdvantageDelta}(x)\geq\tau_{\mathrm{advantage}}\\
&\wedge\ \mathrm{RiskTier}(x)\notin\{\mathrm{PROHIBITED}\}\\
&\wedge\ \mathrm{ECI}(x)\geq\tau_{\mathrm{evidence\_min}} .
\end{aligned}
\]

When triggered, RSI executes: recognize, reproduce, stress-test,
persistence gate, and dossier packaging. Recognition records novelty
distance, advantage delta, risk score, ECI, baseline comparison, archive
cell, and lineage. Reproduction reruns the candidate and
incumbent/neighbor/null baselines under fixed seeds. Stress testing
applies policy shocks, perturbations, adversarial probes, alternate
seeds, and side-effect scans. Persistence requires positive advantage
over baselines under minimum shocks and replays. Dossier packaging emits
a decision-grade breakthrough dossier. High novelty does not lower the
burden of proof; it raises it.

\subsubsection{Baseline discipline: no advantage without
comparators}\label{baseline-discipline-no-advantage-without-comparators}

Mandatory baselines are:

\begin{longtable}[]{@{}
  >{\raggedright\arraybackslash}p{(\columnwidth - 2\tabcolsep) * \real{0.5000}}
  >{\raggedright\arraybackslash}p{(\columnwidth - 2\tabcolsep) * \real{0.5000}}@{}}
\toprule\noalign{}
\begin{minipage}[b]{\linewidth}\raggedright
Baseline
\end{minipage} & \begin{minipage}[b]{\linewidth}\raggedright
Comparator
\end{minipage} \\
\midrule\noalign{}
\endhead
\bottomrule\noalign{}
\endlastfoot
B0 null & No agentic intervention, random policy, or trivial policy. \\
B1 incumbent & Current best validated artifact in the same archive
cell. \\
B2 nearest-neighbor & Best artifact in adjacent descriptor cells. \\
B3 static workflow & Hand-designed or fixed pipeline. \\
B4 single strongest agent & Strong one-model / one-agent baseline. \\
B5 current AGI ALPHA stack & Existing routed, validator-gated system
before the new RSI candidate. \\
\end{longtable}

Promotion requires positive advantage against relevant baselines,
cost-adjusted improvement, safety no worse than incumbent, replayability
complete, and no critical policy violation.

\[
\begin{aligned}
\mathrm{AdvantageDelta}(x,b)=&
\ \mathrm{VerifiedValue}(x)-\mathrm{VerifiedValue}(b)\\
&-\lambda\big(\mathrm{Cost}(x)-\mathrm{Cost}(b)\big)\\
&-\rho\big(\mathrm{Risk}(x)-\mathrm{Risk}(b)\big)\\
&-\kappa\big(\mathrm{CoordinationOverhead}(x)-\mathrm{CoordinationOverhead}(b)\big).
\end{aligned}
\]

\subsubsection{OMNI as allocation, not
authority}\label{omni-as-allocation-not-authority}

OMNI-style interestingness, novelty, and human-notion models are
valuable for directing exploration, but they are not validators. OMNI
may prioritize archive cells, propose bridge targets, select
underexplored niches, generate interesting tasks, recommend probe-first
candidates, identify boring or redundant candidates, and suggest
mutation pressure. OMNI may not insert candidates into the archive,
bypass risk filters, inflate ECI, approve settlement, override
baselines, promote high-novelty candidates, or authorize deployment.

\[
\begin{aligned}
\mathrm{OutcomeAuthority}(x)=&
\ \mathrm{RiskGate}(x)
\wedge \mathrm{EvidenceGate}(x)
\wedge \mathrm{BaselineGate}(x)\\
&\wedge \mathrm{PersistenceGate}(x)
\wedge \mathrm{ReplayGate}(x)
\wedge \mathrm{ValidatorGate}(x).
\end{aligned}
\]

OMNI is not part of OutcomeAuthority except as optional allocation
input.

\subsubsection{RSI dossiers: packaging breakthroughs as institutional
artifacts}\label{rsi-dossiers-packaging-breakthroughs-as-institutional-artifacts}

RSI turns invention outputs into institutional artifacts. It defines
four dossier classes:

\begin{longtable}[]{@{}
  >{\raggedright\arraybackslash}p{(\columnwidth - 2\tabcolsep) * \real{0.5000}}
  >{\raggedright\arraybackslash}p{(\columnwidth - 2\tabcolsep) * \real{0.5000}}@{}}
\toprule\noalign{}
\begin{minipage}[b]{\linewidth}\raggedright
Dossier
\end{minipage} & \begin{minipage}[b]{\linewidth}\raggedright
Use
\end{minipage} \\
\midrule\noalign{}
\endhead
\bottomrule\noalign{}
\endlastfoot
Insight Dossier & Strategic narrative, opportunity framing, early
evidence, open questions, and next tests. \\
MARK Dossier & Audit-heavy technical dossier with reproducibility
checklists, baselines, compliance posture, evidence objects, and replay
instructions. \\
Sovereign Dossier & Institutional dossier covering governance boundary,
security posture, resource implications, policy constraints, and
strategic relevance. \\
Architect / Validator Council Dossier & Highest-assurance dossier
containing independent validation, adversarial review, process-resolved
evidence, semi-formal checks, and deployment authority review. \\
\end{longtable}

\[
\begin{aligned}
\mathrm{RSIDossier}=(&
\mathrm{dossier\_id},\mathrm{candidate\_id},\mathrm{archive\_cell},
\mathrm{novelty\_distance},\mathrm{advantage\_delta},\\
&\mathrm{baselines},\mathrm{reproduction\_manifest},
\mathrm{stress\_tests},\mathrm{evidence\_objects},
\mathrm{eci\_summary},\\
&\mathrm{risk\_report},\mathrm{causal\_atlas\_links},
\mathrm{proof\_bundle\_refs},
\mathrm{validator\_attestations},\\
&\mathrm{promotion\_decision},\mathrm{governance\_notes},
\mathrm{replay\_instructions},
\mathrm{public\_safe\_summary},\\
&\mathrm{private\_audit\_appendix})
\end{aligned}
\]

No Move-37 claim without a dossier. No strategic promotion without a
dossier. No institutional deployment without replayable dossier
evidence.

\subsubsection{RSI state-capacity
advantage}\label{rsi-state-capacity-advantage}

AGI Alpha RSI does not merely improve model capability. It improves
institutional state capacity for machine labor.

\begin{longtable}[]{@{}
  >{\raggedright\arraybackslash}p{(\columnwidth - 2\tabcolsep) * \real{0.5000}}
  >{\raggedright\arraybackslash}p{(\columnwidth - 2\tabcolsep) * \real{0.5000}}@{}}
\toprule\noalign{}
\begin{minipage}[b]{\linewidth}\raggedright
Dimension
\end{minipage} & \begin{minipage}[b]{\linewidth}\raggedright
RSI meaning
\end{minipage} \\
\midrule\noalign{}
\endhead
\bottomrule\noalign{}
\endlastfoot
Legibility & Replayability, schemas, proof bundles, evidence logs, and
audit trails. \\
Control & Mechanical gates, authority boundaries, risk routing, pause
controls, and no OMNI outcome authority. \\
Continuity & Append-only ledgers, persistent archive, scaffold lineages,
causal atlas memory, and drift sentinel. \\
Coordination & Dossiers, schema-bound artifacts, baseline libraries,
validator councils, MandateEpochs, AGI Jobs, and AGI Nodes. \\
Compounding & Stepping-stone retention, lineage metaproductivity, QD
archive coverage, regression detection, and reinvestment policy. \\
\end{longtable}

Define compact factors:

\[
\begin{aligned}
A_{\mathrm{RSI}} &=
\mathrm{Legibility}\cdot\mathrm{Control}\cdot\mathrm{Continuity}
\cdot\mathrm{Coordination}\cdot\mathrm{Compounding},\\
B_{\mathrm{RSI}} &=
\mathrm{CoordinationCost}+\mathrm{AuditCost}+\mathrm{GovernanceLatency}\\
&\quad+\mathrm{DriftRisk}+\mathrm{FalsePromotionRisk},\\
D_{\mathrm{RSI\_capacity}} &= \frac{A_{\mathrm{RSI}}}{B_{\mathrm{RSI}}}.
\end{aligned}
\]

The civilizational governance metric becomes:

\[
\begin{aligned}
A_{\mathrm{civ,RSI}} &=
D_{\mathrm{civ++}}\cdot D_{\mathrm{RSI\_capacity}}
\cdot\mathrm{ReplayabilityRate}\\
&\quad\cdot\mathrm{ExecutedEvidenceShare}
\cdot\mathrm{BaselineDisciplineScore}
\cdot\mathrm{PersistenceIntegrity},\\
B_{\mathrm{civ,RSI}} &=
1+\mathrm{DriftRisk}+\mathrm{EvidenceInflationRisk}\\
&\quad+\mathrm{NoveltyMillRisk}+\mathrm{DossierDebt},\\
D_{\mathrm{civ,RSI}} &= \frac{A_{\mathrm{civ,RSI}}}{B_{\mathrm{civ,RSI}}}.
\end{aligned}
\]

\subsubsection{RSI complements frontier labs - it does not imitate
them}\label{rsi-complements-frontier-labs---it-does-not-imitate-them}

Frontier labs optimize for capability velocity. RSI optimizes for
durable, auditable compounding advantage under governance. A frontier
sprint emphasizes rapid prototypes, taste-driven iteration, and
breakthrough chasing. A governed sprint emphasizes fast probes, hard
gates, and reproducible deltas. Legacy bureaucracy has slow approvals,
weak measurement, and low compounding. AGI Alpha RSI combines
deterministic replay, evidence-first promotion, sovereign dossiers, and
append-only compounding memory. The claim is not that RSI replaces
frontier labs; it claims that frontier capability without a
deterministic invention governance institution is difficult to
underwrite, audit, or safely compound.

\subsubsection{Strategic enabling
infrastructure}\label{strategic-enabling-infrastructure}

AGI Alpha RSI is strategic enabling infrastructure for intelligence
organizations. It raises the return and safety of downstream AI programs
by ensuring that invention outputs are reproducible, validated, audited,
and governable before they become capital, infrastructure, or deployment
decisions. The point is durable governance of invention, not
uncontrolled strategic escalation.

\subsubsection{RSI Evidence Docket: from architecture to real-task
proof}\label{rsi-evidence-docket-from-architecture-to-real-task-proof}

AGI ALPHA must not claim scalable, efficient, safe multi-agent
coordination unless an RSI Evidence Docket exists.

\begin{Shaded}
\begin{Highlighting}[]
\NormalTok{rsi{-}evidence{-}docket/}
\NormalTok{  00\_claims\_matrix.md}
\NormalTok{  01\_runner\_manifest.json}
\NormalTok{  02\_prompt\_pack\_hashes.json}
\NormalTok{  03\_state\_hashes.json}
\NormalTok{  04\_task\_manifests/}
\NormalTok{  05\_baselines/}
\NormalTok{  06\_agialpha\_rsi\_runs/}
\NormalTok{  07\_microbench\_results/}
\NormalTok{  08\_evidence\_objects/}
\NormalTok{  09\_eci\_ledger/}
\NormalTok{  10\_proof\_bundles/}
\NormalTok{  11\_baseline\_comparisons/}
\NormalTok{  12\_move37\_dossiers/}
\NormalTok{  13\_safety\_ledgers/}
\NormalTok{  14\_cost\_ledgers/}
\NormalTok{  15\_replay\_instructions/}
\NormalTok{  16\_independent\_replay\_reports/}
\NormalTok{  17\_summary\_tables/}
\end{Highlighting}
\end{Shaded}

Every empirical coordination claim must answer: what real task was
performed; which agents participated; which scaffolds were active; which
tools were used; what baseline was used; what evidence was executed;
what was replayed; what cost was incurred; what safety profile resulted;
what AdvantageDelta was observed; what persisted into the archive; and
what the system learned for the next cycle.

\textbf{Rule:} no Evidence Docket, no empirical SOTA claim.

\subsubsection{Commercial independence and publication-safe claim
boundary}\label{commercial-independence-and-publication-safe-claim-boundary}

AGI Alpha RSI Integration, AGI\_Alpha\_RSI\_Sovereign\_v0, and
AGI\_Alpha\_RSI\_Sovereign\_Strategy\_Brief\_v0 are used as internal
strategic and technical architecture sources. External works referenced
in those materials are cited only as scientific inspiration and
prior-art context. AGI ALPHA develops its own commercially independent
RSI control plane: deterministic runner semantics, schema-bound prompt
ecosystem, ECI ledger, drift sentinel, QD archive, OMNI allocation
controls, Move-37 breakthrough handling, baseline library, ProofBundles,
alpha-Work Units, MandateEpoch settlement, sovereign dossiers, and
evidence-docket benchmarks.

The paper does not claim achieved superintelligence, achieved ASI,
autonomous sovereignty, guaranteed market dominance, energy abundance,
or civilization-scale capability. It claims a testable architecture: a
deterministic, validator-gated, market-governed, recursively improving
intelligence-organization substrate whose outputs become empirical only
through executed evidence, replayable ProofBundles, baseline
comparisons, safety ledgers, cost/risk accounting, delayed outcomes, and
independent audit.

\subsection{Value Capture, Capital Formation, and Reinvestment
Governance}\label{value-capture-capital-formation-and-reinvestment-governance}

The civilizational objective depends not only on capability, but on
ownership, value capture, and disciplined reinvestment. The paper
therefore does not stop at ``agents do work.'' It models how work
becomes owned capability and how owned capability compounds.

\textbf{Value Capture Ledger.} Tracks how accepted evidence bundles
become revenue, intellectual property, internal tools, cost reductions,
infrastructure plans, scientific assets, market mechanisms, or strategic
capabilities.

\textbf{Reinvestment Policy.} Allocates verified gains into compute,
data, tooling, security, validator capacity, research, robotics,
laboratories, energy systems, and strategic reserves.

\textbf{Invention Reserve.} Stores non-commoditized, high-leverage
discoveries whose best use is internal compounding.

\textbf{Capability Monetization Boundary.} Determines whether a
capability should be sold, licensed, kept internal, open-sourced,
sandboxed, or retired.

Capital formation is measured by:

\[
\begin{aligned}
K_{\mathrm{gain}}={}&
\mathrm{revenue}_{\mathrm{gain}}
+\mathrm{cost}_{\mathrm{reduction}}
+\mathrm{asset}_{\mathrm{value}} \\
&+\mathrm{option}_{\mathrm{strategic}}
+\mathrm{infrastructure}_{\mathrm{value}} \\
&-R_{\mathrm{legal}}-R_{\mathrm{safety}}-R_{\mathrm{concentration}}.
\end{aligned}
\]

Reinvestment efficiency is:

\[
\eta_{\mathrm{reinvest}}
=
\frac{
\Delta\!\big(W_{\mathrm{verified}}+C_{\mathrm{compute}}+E_{\mathrm{useful}}
+S_{\mathrm{science}}+I_{\mathrm{infrastructure}}\big)
}{K_{\mathrm{reinvested}}}.
\]

A superintelligent invention engine would be valuable only if its
outputs can be captured, governed, reinvested, and compounded without
creating unacceptable systemic risk.

\subsection{Frontier layers as flywheel
components}\label{frontier-layers-as-flywheel-components}

Every frontier layer serves the value-to-energy flywheel.

\begin{longtable}[]{@{}
  >{\raggedright\arraybackslash}p{(\columnwidth - 2\tabcolsep) * \real{0.5000}}
  >{\raggedright\arraybackslash}p{(\columnwidth - 2\tabcolsep) * \real{0.5000}}@{}}
\toprule\noalign{}
\begin{minipage}[b]{\linewidth}\raggedright
Layer
\end{minipage} & \begin{minipage}[b]{\linewidth}\raggedright
Role in the flywheel
\end{minipage} \\
\midrule\noalign{}
\endhead
\bottomrule\noalign{}
\endlastfoot
Learned coordination & Turns many models/agents into one organized labor
system. \\
Experience streams & Converts actions and outcomes into training
material. \\
ProofZero planning & Searches future organizational actions before
spending real resources. \\
Directed evolution / DISCO analogy & Shows proposal -\textgreater{}
validation -\textgreater{} lineage -\textgreater{} improvement. \\
Sovereign Evolutionary Agent Economy & Allocates jobs, compute,
validators, rewards, and market permeability. \\
Synthetic curricula & Generates new task frontiers from task
definitions. \\
Lineage metaproductivity & Rewards descendants that create better future
capabilities. \\
Dynamic verifiable evolution & Turns open-problem search into reusable
learning. \\

settleable work. \\

packaging, validation, sentinels, and observability. \\
Proof bundles & Convert outputs into settlement-grade evidence. \\
α-Work Units & Convert verified work into a canonical accounting
unit. \\
Chronicle & Converts completed jobs into durable public/institutional
memory. \\
\$AGIALPHA & Stakes, settles, and coordinates protocol operations
without implying equity or profit rights. \\
MontrealAI GitHub corpus & Supplies public implementation scaffolds,
local/devnet demos, CI gates, runbooks, contracts, nodes, and
proof-first release surfaces that can be converted into benchmark
evidence dockets. \\
\end{longtable}

\subsection{Mechanisms mapped to the Kardashev-aligned
flywheel}\label{mechanisms-mapped-to-the-kardashev-aligned-flywheel}

A cited work or mechanism is admissible only if it becomes a mechanism,
metric, experiment, design constraint, governance control, or
implementation requirement that improves the safe conversion of
intelligence into compounding productive capacity.

\begin{longtable}[]{@{}
  >{\raggedright\arraybackslash}p{(\columnwidth - 2\tabcolsep) * \real{0.5000}}
  >{\raggedright\arraybackslash}p{(\columnwidth - 2\tabcolsep) * \real{0.5000}}@{}}
\toprule\noalign{}
\begin{minipage}[b]{\linewidth}\raggedright
Mechanism
\end{minipage} & \begin{minipage}[b]{\linewidth}\raggedright
Role in the Kardashev-aligned flywheel
\end{minipage} \\
\midrule\noalign{}
\endhead
\bottomrule\noalign{}
\endlastfoot
Subversion-Resistant Validation & Prevents strategically deceptive
agents from converting hidden failure, backdoors, collusion, or unsafe
artifacts into accepted work, protecting the capital and infrastructure
flywheel. \\
Process-Resolved Evidence Validation & Turns final-output validation
into stepwise due diligence, making machine labor investable, auditable,
insurable, and reusable. \\
Proof-Native Agent Workbench & Converts software repair, code
generation, testing, rollback, and deployment into reproducible
proof-bearing engineering labor. \\

interactive environments before claims are made about real-world
productivity. \\

operational assets that compound future work. \\

without immediate weight updates. \\
